<s> the canal overflowed in the garden behind the rising waters on either side at last burst open the doors and meeting in the house rose to the height of six feet <\s>
<s> it was a picturesque sight at night to see the peasants driving the cattle from the plains below to the hills above the baths <\s>
<s> a fire was kept up to guide them across the ford and the forms of the men and the animals showed in dark relief against the red glare of the flame which was reflected again in the waters that filled the square <\s>
<s> we then removed to pisa and took up our abode there for the winter <\s>
<s> the extreme mildness of the climate suited shelley and his solitude was enlivened by an intercourse with several intimate friends <\s>
<s> chance cast us strangely enough on this quiet half unpeopled town but its very peace suited shelley <\s>
<s> its river the near mountains and not distant sea added to its attractions and were the objects of many delightful excursions <\s>
<s> we feared the south of italy and a hotter climate on account of our child our former bereavement inspiring us with terror <\s>
<s> we seemed to take root here and moved little afterwards often indeed entertaining projects for visiting other parts of italy but still delaying <\s>
<s> but for our fears on account of our child i believe we should have wandered over the world both being passionately fond of travelling <\s>
<s> but human life besides its great unalterable necessities is ruled by a thousand lilliputian ties that shackle at the time although it is difficult to account afterwards for their influence over our destiny <\s>
<s> poems written in 1821 <\s>
<s> dirge for the year <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 and dated january 1 1821 1 <\s>
<s> orphan hours the year is dead come and sigh come and weep <\s>
<s> merry hours smile instead for the year is but asleep <\s>
<s> see it smiles as it is sleeping 5 mocking your untimely weeping <\s>
<s> as an earthquake rocks a corse in its coffin in the clay so white winter that rough nurse rocks the death cold year to day 10 solemn hours <\s>
<s> wail aloud for your mother in her shroud <\s>
<s> as the wild air stirs and sways the tree swung cradle of a child so the breath of these rude days 15 rocks the year be calm and mild trembling hours she will arise with new love within her eyes <\s>
<s> january gray is here like a sexton by her grave 20 february bears the bier march with grief doth howl and rave and april weeps but o ye hours <\s>
<s> follow with may's fairest flowers <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> swiftly walk o'er the western wave spirit of night <\s>
<s> out of the misty eastern cave where all the long and lone daylight thou wovest dreams of joy and fear 5 which make thee terrible and dear swift be thy flight <\s>
<s> wrap thy form in a mantle gray star inwrought <\s>
<s> blind with thine hair the eyes of day 10 kiss her until she be wearied out then wander o'er city and sea and land touching all with thine opiate wand come long sought <\s>
<s> when i arose and saw the dawn 15 i sighed for thee when light rode high and the dew was gone and noon lay heavy on flower and tree and the weary day turned to his rest lingering like an unloved guest i sighed for thee <\s>
<s> thy brother death came and cried wouldst thou me <\s>
<s> thy sweet child sleep the filmy eyed murmured like a noontide bee 25 shall i nestle near thy side <\s>
<s> wouldst thou me and i replied no not thee <\s>
<s> death will come when thou art dead soon too soon 30 sleep will come when thou art fled of neither would i ask the boon i ask of thee beloved night swift be thine approaching flight come soon soon <\s>
<s> 35 note 1 o'er harvard manuscript over editions 1824 1839 <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> whose waves are years ocean of time whose waters of deep woe are brackish with the salt of human tears <\s>
<s> thou shoreless flood which in thy ebb and flow claspest the limits of mortality 5 and sick of prey yet howling on for more vomitest thy wrecks on its inhospitable shore treacherous in calm and terrible in storm who shall put forth on thee unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 1 <\s>
<s> far far away o ye halcyons of memory seek some far calmer nest than this abandoned breast <\s>
<s> no news of your false spring 5 to my heart's winter bring once having gone in vain ye come again <\s>
<s> vultures who build your bowers high in the future's towers 10 withered hopes on hopes are spread <\s>
<s> dying joys choked by the dead will serve your beaks for prey many a day <\s>
<s> from the arabic an imitation <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is an intermediate draft amongst the bodleian manuscripts <\s>
<s> see locock examination etc 1903 page 13 1 <\s>
<s> my faint spirit was sitting in the light of thy looks my love it panted for thee like the hind at noon for the brooks my love <\s>
<s> thy barb whose hoofs outspeed the tempest's flight 5 bore thee far from me my heart for my weak feet were weary soon did companion thee <\s>
<s> fleeter far than fleetest storm or steed or the death they bear 10 the heart which tender thought clothes like a dove with the wings of care in the battle in the darkness in the need shall mine cling to thee nor claim one smile for all the comfort love 15 it may bring to thee <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 2 1 by dr <\s>
<s> garnett relics of shelley 1862 2 2 and 3 by h <\s>
<s> buxton forman poetical works of p <\s>
<s> madonna wherefore hast thou sent to me sweet basil and mignonette <\s>
<s> embleming love and health which never yet in the same wreath might be <\s>
<s> alas and they are wet <\s>
<s> 5 is it with thy kisses or thy tears <\s>
<s> for never rain or dew such fragrance drew from plant or flower the very doubt endears my sadness ever new 10 the sighs i breathe the tears i shed for thee <\s>
<s> send the stars light but send not love to me in whom love ever made health like a heap of embers soon to fade the fugitives <\s>
<s> the waters are flashing the white hail is dashing the lightnings are glancing the hoar spray is dancing away <\s>
<s> 5 the whirlwind is rolling the thunder is tolling the forest is swinging the minster bells ringing come away <\s>
<s> 10 the earth is like ocean wreck strewn and in motion bird beast man and worm have crept out of the storm come away <\s>
<s> our boat has one sail and the helmsman is pale a bold pilot i trow who should follow us now shouted he 20 and she cried ply the oar <\s>
<s> put off gaily from shore as she spoke bolts of death mixed with hail specked their path o'er the sea <\s>
<s> 25 and from isle tower and rock the blue beacon cloud broke and though dumb in the blast the red cannon flashed fast from the lee <\s>
<s> and drive we not free o'er the terrible sea i and thou <\s>
<s> 35 one boat cloak did cover the loved and the lover their blood beats one measure they murmur proud pleasure soft and low 40 while around the lashed ocean like mountains in motion is withdrawn and uplifted sunk shattered and shifted to and fro <\s>
<s> in the court of the fortress beside the pale portress like a bloodhound well beaten the bridegroom stands eaten by shame 50 on the topmost watch turret as a death boding spirit stands the gray tyrant father to his voice the mad weather seems tame 55 and with curses as wild as e'er clung to child he devotes to the blast the best loveliest and last of his name <\s>
<s> 60 notes 28 and though though editions 1839 <\s>
<s> 57 clung cling editions 1839 <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 music when soft voices die vibrates in the memory odours when sweet violets sicken live within the sense they quicken <\s>
<s> rose leaves when the rose is dead 5 are heaped for the beloved's bed and so thy thoughts when thou art gone love itself shall slumber on <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> rarely rarely comest thou spirit of delight <\s>
<s> wherefore hast thou left me now many a day and night <\s>
<s> many a weary night and day 5 tis since thou art fled away <\s>
<s> how shall ever one like me win thee back again <\s>
<s> with the joyous and the free thou wilt scoff at pain <\s>
<s> thou hast forgot all but those who need thee not <\s>
<s> as a lizard with the shade of a trembling leaf thou with sorrow art dismayed 15 even the sighs of grief reproach thee that thou art not near and reproach thou wilt not hear <\s>
<s> let me set my mournful ditty to a merry measure 20 thou wilt never come for pity thou wilt come for pleasure pity then will cut away those cruel wings and thou wilt stay <\s>
<s> i love all that thou lovest 25 spirit of delight <\s>
<s> the fresh earth in new leaves dressed and the starry night autumn evening and the morn when the golden mists are born <\s>
<s> i love snow and all the forms of the radiant frost i love waves and winds and storms everything almost which is nature's and may be 35 untainted by man's misery <\s>
<s> i love tranquil solitude and such society as is quiet wise and good between thee and me 40 what difference <\s>
<s> but thou dost possess the things i seek not love them less <\s>
<s> i love love though he has wings and like light can flee but above all other things 45 spirit i love thee thou art love and life <\s>
<s> oh come make once more my heart thy home <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>

<s> the flower that smiles to day to morrow dies all that we wish to stay tempts and then flies <\s>
<s> what is this world's delight <\s>
<s> 5 lightning that mocks the night brief even as bright <\s>
<s> virtue how frail it is <\s>
<s> love how it sells poor bliss 10 for proud despair <\s>
<s> but we though soon they fall survive their joy and all which ours we call <\s>

<s> rarely rarely comest thou spirit of delight <\s>
<s> wherefore hast thou left me now many a day and night <\s>
<s> many a weary night and day 5 tis since thou art fled away <\s>
<s> how shall ever one like me win thee back again <\s>
<s> with the joyous and the free thou wilt scoff at pain <\s>
<s> thou hast forgot all but those who need thee not <\s>
<s> as a lizard with the shade of a trembling leaf thou with sorrow art dismayed 15 even the sighs of grief reproach thee that thou art not near and reproach thou wilt not hear <\s>
<s> let me set my mournful ditty to a merry measure 20 thou wilt never come for pity thou wilt come for pleasure pity then will cut away those cruel wings and thou wilt stay <\s>
<s> i love all that thou lovest 25 spirit of delight <\s>
<s> the fresh earth in new leaves dressed and the starry night autumn evening and the morn when the golden mists are born <\s>
<s> i love snow and all the forms of the radiant frost i love waves and winds and storms everything almost which is nature's and may be 35 untainted by man's misery <\s>
<s> i love tranquil solitude and such society as is quiet wise and good between thee and me 40 what difference <\s>
<s> but thou dost possess the things i seek not love them less <\s>
<s> i love love though he has wings and like light can flee but above all other things 45 spirit i love thee thou art love and life <\s>
<s> oh come make once more my heart thy home <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a fair draft amongst the boscombe manuscripts 1 <\s>
<s> the flower that smiles to day to morrow dies all that we wish to stay tempts and then flies <\s>
<s> what is this world's delight <\s>
<s> 5 lightning that mocks the night brief even as bright <\s>
<s> virtue how frail it is <\s>
<s> love how it sells poor bliss 10 for proud despair <\s>
<s> but we though soon they fall survive their joy and all which ours we call <\s>
<s> the canal overflowed in the garden behind the rising waters on either side at last burst open the doors and meeting in the house rose to the height of six feet <\s>
<s> it was a picturesque sight at night to see the peasants driving the cattle from the plains below to the hills above the baths <\s>
<s> a fire was kept up to guide them across the ford and the forms of the men and the animals showed in dark relief against the red glare of the flame which was reflected again in the waters that filled the square <\s>
<s> we then removed to pisa and took up our abode there for the winter <\s>
<s> the extreme mildness of the climate suited shelley and his solitude was enlivened by an intercourse with several intimate friends <\s>
<s> chance cast us strangely enough on this quiet half unpeopled town but its very peace suited shelley <\s>
<s> its river the near mountains and not distant sea added to its attractions and were the objects of many delightful excursions <\s>
<s> we feared the south of italy and a hotter climate on account of our child our former bereavement inspiring us with terror <\s>
<s> we seemed to take root here and moved little afterwards often indeed entertaining projects for visiting other parts of italy but still delaying <\s>
<s> but for our fears on account of our child i believe we should have wandered over the world both being passionately fond of travelling <\s>
<s> but human life besides its great unalterable necessities is ruled by a thousand lilliputian ties that shackle at the time although it is difficult to account afterwards for their influence over our destiny <\s>
<s> poems written in 1821 <\s>
<s> dirge for the year <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 and dated january 1 1821 1 <\s>
<s> orphan hours the year is dead come and sigh come and weep <\s>
<s> merry hours smile instead for the year is but asleep <\s>
<s> see it smiles as it is sleeping 5 mocking your untimely weeping <\s>
<s> as an earthquake rocks a corse in its coffin in the clay so white winter that rough nurse rocks the death cold year to day 10 solemn hours <\s>
<s> wail aloud for your mother in her shroud <\s>
<s> as the wild air stirs and sways the tree swung cradle of a child so the breath of these rude days 15 rocks the year be calm and mild trembling hours she will arise with new love within her eyes <\s>
<s> january gray is here like a sexton by her grave 20 february bears the bier march with grief doth howl and rave and april weeps but o ye hours <\s>
<s> follow with may's fairest flowers <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> swiftly walk o'er the western wave spirit of night <\s>
<s> out of the misty eastern cave where all the long and lone daylight thou wovest dreams of joy and fear 5 which make thee terrible and dear swift be thy flight <\s>
<s> wrap thy form in a mantle gray star inwrought <\s>
<s> blind with thine hair the eyes of day 10 kiss her until she be wearied out then wander o'er city and sea and land touching all with thine opiate wand come long sought <\s>
<s> when i arose and saw the dawn 15 i sighed for thee when light rode high and the dew was gone and noon lay heavy on flower and tree and the weary day turned to his rest lingering like an unloved guest i sighed for thee <\s>
<s> thy brother death came and cried wouldst thou me <\s>
<s> thy sweet child sleep the filmy eyed murmured like a noontide bee 25 shall i nestle near thy side <\s>
<s> wouldst thou me and i replied no not thee <\s>
<s> death will come when thou art dead soon too soon 30 sleep will come when thou art fled of neither would i ask the boon i ask of thee beloved night swift be thine approaching flight come soon soon <\s>
<s> 35 note 1 o'er harvard manuscript over editions 1824 1839 <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> whose waves are years ocean of time whose waters of deep woe are brackish with the salt of human tears <\s>
<s> thou shoreless flood which in thy ebb and flow claspest the limits of mortality 5 and sick of prey yet howling on for more vomitest thy wrecks on its inhospitable shore treacherous in calm and terrible in storm who shall put forth on thee unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 1 <\s>
<s> far far away o ye halcyons of memory seek some far calmer nest than this abandoned breast <\s>
<s> no news of your false spring 5 to my heart's winter bring once having gone in vain ye come again <\s>
<s> vultures who build your bowers high in the future's towers 10 withered hopes on hopes are spread <\s>
<s> dying joys choked by the dead will serve your beaks for prey many a day <\s>
<s> from the arabic an imitation <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is an intermediate draft amongst the bodleian manuscripts <\s>
<s> see locock examination etc 1903 page 13 1 <\s>
<s> my faint spirit was sitting in the light of thy looks my love it panted for thee like the hind at noon for the brooks my love <\s>
<s> thy barb whose hoofs outspeed the tempest's flight 5 bore thee far from me my heart for my weak feet were weary soon did companion thee <\s>
<s> fleeter far than fleetest storm or steed or the death they bear 10 the heart which tender thought clothes like a dove with the wings of care in the battle in the darkness in the need shall mine cling to thee nor claim one smile for all the comfort love 15 it may bring to thee <\s>
<s> notes 3 hoofs feet b <\s>
<s> 7 were grew b <\s>
<s> 9 ah o b <\s>
<s> published 1 by mrs <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 2 1 by dr <\s>
<s> garnett relics of shelley 1862 2 2 and 3 by h <\s>
<s> buxton forman poetical works of p <\s>
<s> madonna wherefore hast thou sent to me sweet basil and mignonette <\s>
<s> embleming love and health which never yet in the same wreath might be <\s>
<s> alas and they are wet <\s>
<s> 5 is it with thy kisses or thy tears <\s>
<s> for never rain or dew such fragrance drew from plant or flower the very doubt endears my sadness ever new 10 the sighs i breathe the tears i shed for thee <\s>
<s> send the stars light but send not love to me in whom love ever made health like a heap of embers soon to fade the fugitives <\s>
<s> the waters are flashing the white hail is dashing the lightnings are glancing the hoar spray is dancing away <\s>
<s> 5 the whirlwind is rolling the thunder is tolling the forest is swinging the minster bells ringing come away <\s>
<s> 10 the earth is like ocean wreck strewn and in motion bird beast man and worm have crept out of the storm come away <\s>
<s> our boat has one sail and the helmsman is pale a bold pilot i trow who should follow us now shouted he 20 and she cried ply the oar <\s>
<s> put off gaily from shore as she spoke bolts of death mixed with hail specked their path o'er the sea <\s>
<s> 25 and from isle tower and rock the blue beacon cloud broke and though dumb in the blast the red cannon flashed fast from the lee <\s>
<s> and drive we not free o'er the terrible sea i and thou <\s>
<s> 35 one boat cloak did cover the loved and the lover their blood beats one measure they murmur proud pleasure soft and low 40 while around the lashed ocean like mountains in motion is withdrawn and uplifted sunk shattered and shifted to and fro <\s>
<s> in the court of the fortress beside the pale portress like a bloodhound well beaten the bridegroom stands eaten by shame 50 on the topmost watch turret as a death boding spirit stands the gray tyrant father to his voice the mad weather seems tame 55 and with curses as wild as e'er clung to child he devotes to the blast the best loveliest and last of his name <\s>
<s> 60 notes 28 and though though editions 1839 <\s>
<s> 57 clung cling editions 1839 <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 music when soft voices die vibrates in the memory odours when sweet violets sicken live within the sense they quicken <\s>
<s> rose leaves when the rose is dead 5 are heaped for the beloved's bed and so thy thoughts when thou art gone love itself shall slumber on <\s>

<s> 5 is it with thy kisses or thy tears <\s>
<s> for never rain or dew such fragrance drew from plant or flower the very doubt endears my sadness ever new 10 the sighs i breathe the tears i shed for thee <\s>
<s> send the stars light but send not love to me in whom love ever made health like a heap of embers soon to fade the fugitives <\s>
<s> the waters are flashing the white hail is dashing the lightnings are glancing the hoar spray is dancing away <\s>
<s> 5 the whirlwind is rolling the thunder is tolling the forest is swinging the minster bells ringing come away <\s>
<s> 10 the earth is like ocean wreck strewn and in motion bird beast man and worm have crept out of the storm come away <\s>
<s> our boat has one sail and the helmsman is pale a bold pilot i trow who should follow us now shouted he 20 and she cried ply the oar <\s>
<s> put off gaily from shore as she spoke bolts of death mixed with hail specked their path o'er the sea <\s>
<s> 25 and from isle tower and rock the blue beacon cloud broke and though dumb in the blast the red cannon flashed fast from the lee <\s>
<s> and drive we not free o'er the terrible sea i and thou <\s>
<s> 35 one boat cloak did cover the loved and the lover their blood beats one measure they murmur proud pleasure soft and low 40 while around the lashed ocean like mountains in motion is withdrawn and uplifted sunk shattered and shifted to and fro <\s>
<s> in the court of the fortress beside the pale portress like a bloodhound well beaten the bridegroom stands eaten by shame 50 on the topmost watch turret as a death boding spirit stands the gray tyrant father to his voice the mad weather seems tame 55 and with curses as wild as e'er clung to child he devotes to the blast the best loveliest and last of his name <\s>

<s> 57 clung cling editions 1839 <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 music when soft voices die vibrates in the memory odours when sweet violets sicken live within the sense they quicken <\s>
<s> rose leaves when the rose is dead 5 are heaped for the beloved's bed and so thy thoughts when thou art gone love itself shall slumber on <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> rarely rarely comest thou spirit of delight <\s>
<s> wherefore hast thou left me now many a day and night <\s>
<s> many a weary night and day 5 tis since thou art fled away <\s>
<s> how shall ever one like me win thee back again <\s>
<s> with the joyous and the free thou wilt scoff at pain <\s>
<s> thou hast forgot all but those who need thee not <\s>
<s> as a lizard with the shade of a trembling leaf thou with sorrow art dismayed 15 even the sighs of grief reproach thee that thou art not near and reproach thou wilt not hear <\s>
<s> let me set my mournful ditty to a merry measure 20 thou wilt never come for pity thou wilt come for pleasure pity then will cut away those cruel wings and thou wilt stay <\s>
<s> i love all that thou lovest 25 spirit of delight <\s>
<s> the fresh earth in new leaves dressed and the starry night autumn evening and the morn when the golden mists are born <\s>
<s> i love snow and all the forms of the radiant frost i love waves and winds and storms everything almost which is nature's and may be 35 untainted by man's misery <\s>
<s> i love tranquil solitude and such society as is quiet wise and good between thee and me 40 what difference <\s>
<s> but thou dost possess the things i seek not love them less <\s>
<s> i love love though he has wings and like light can flee but above all other things 45 spirit i love thee thou art love and life <\s>
<s> oh come make once more my heart thy home <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a fair draft amongst the boscombe manuscripts 1 <\s>
<s> the flower that smiles to day to morrow dies all that we wish to stay tempts and then flies <\s>
<s> what is this world's delight <\s>
<s> 5 lightning that mocks the night brief even as bright <\s>
<s> virtue how frail it is <\s>
<s> love how it sells poor bliss 10 for proud despair <\s>
<s> but we though soon they fall survive their joy and all which ours we call <\s>
<s> the canal overflowed in the garden behind the rising waters on either side at last burst open the doors and meeting in the house rose to the height of six feet <\s>
<s> it was a picturesque sight at night to see the peasants driving the cattle from the plains below to the hills above the baths <\s>
<s> a fire was kept up to guide them across the ford and the forms of the men and the animals showed in dark relief against the red glare of the flame which was reflected again in the waters that filled the square <\s>
<s> we then removed to pisa and took up our abode there for the winter <\s>
<s> the extreme mildness of the climate suited shelley and his solitude was enlivened by an intercourse with several intimate friends <\s>
<s> chance cast us strangely enough on this quiet half unpeopled town but its very peace suited shelley <\s>
<s> its river the near mountains and not distant sea added to its attractions and were the objects of many delightful excursions <\s>
<s> we feared the south of italy and a hotter climate on account of our child our former bereavement inspiring us with terror <\s>
<s> we seemed to take root here and moved little afterwards often indeed entertaining projects for visiting other parts of italy but still delaying <\s>
<s> but for our fears on account of our child i believe we should have wandered over the world both being passionately fond of travelling <\s>
<s> but human life besides its great unalterable necessities is ruled by a thousand lilliputian ties that shackle at the time although it is difficult to account afterwards for their influence over our destiny <\s>
<s> poems written in 1821 <\s>
<s> dirge for the year <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 and dated january 1 1821 1 <\s>
<s> orphan hours the year is dead come and sigh come and weep <\s>
<s> merry hours smile instead for the year is but asleep <\s>
<s> see it smiles as it is sleeping 5 mocking your untimely weeping <\s>
<s> as an earthquake rocks a corse in its coffin in the clay so white winter that rough nurse rocks the death cold year to day 10 solemn hours <\s>
<s> wail aloud for your mother in her shroud <\s>
<s> as the wild air stirs and sways the tree swung cradle of a child so the breath of these rude days 15 rocks the year be calm and mild trembling hours she will arise with new love within her eyes <\s>
<s> january gray is here like a sexton by her grave 20 february bears the bier march with grief doth howl and rave and april weeps but o ye hours <\s>
<s> follow with may's fairest flowers <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> swiftly walk o'er the western wave spirit of night <\s>
<s> out of the misty eastern cave where all the long and lone daylight thou wovest dreams of joy and fear 5 which make thee terrible and dear swift be thy flight <\s>
<s> wrap thy form in a mantle gray star inwrought <\s>
<s> blind with thine hair the eyes of day 10 kiss her until she be wearied out then wander o'er city and sea and land touching all with thine opiate wand come long sought <\s>
<s> when i arose and saw the dawn 15 i sighed for thee when light rode high and the dew was gone and noon lay heavy on flower and tree and the weary day turned to his rest lingering like an unloved guest i sighed for thee <\s>
<s> thy brother death came and cried wouldst thou me <\s>
<s> thy sweet child sleep the filmy eyed murmured like a noontide bee 25 shall i nestle near thy side <\s>
<s> wouldst thou me and i replied no not thee <\s>
<s> death will come when thou art dead soon too soon 30 sleep will come when thou art fled of neither would i ask the boon i ask of thee beloved night swift be thine approaching flight come soon soon <\s>
<s> 35 note 1 o'er harvard manuscript over editions 1824 1839 <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> whose waves are years ocean of time whose waters of deep woe are brackish with the salt of human tears <\s>
<s> thou shoreless flood which in thy ebb and flow claspest the limits of mortality 5 and sick of prey yet howling on for more vomitest thy wrecks on its inhospitable shore treacherous in calm and terrible in storm who shall put forth on thee unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 1 <\s>
<s> far far away o ye halcyons of memory seek some far calmer nest than this abandoned breast <\s>
<s> no news of your false spring 5 to my heart's winter bring once having gone in vain ye come again <\s>
<s> vultures who build your bowers high in the future's towers 10 withered hopes on hopes are spread <\s>
<s> dying joys choked by the dead will serve your beaks for prey many a day <\s>
<s> from the arabic an imitation <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is an intermediate draft amongst the bodleian manuscripts <\s>
<s> see locock examination etc 1903 page 13 1 <\s>
<s> my faint spirit was sitting in the light of thy looks my love it panted for thee like the hind at noon for the brooks my love <\s>
<s> thy barb whose hoofs outspeed the tempest's flight 5 bore thee far from me my heart for my weak feet were weary soon did companion thee <\s>
<s> fleeter far than fleetest storm or steed or the death they bear 10 the heart which tender thought clothes like a dove with the wings of care in the battle in the darkness in the need shall mine cling to thee nor claim one smile for all the comfort love 15 it may bring to thee <\s>

<s> whose waves are years ocean of time whose waters of deep woe are brackish with the salt of human tears <\s>
<s> thou shoreless flood which in thy ebb and flow claspest the limits of mortality 5 and sick of prey yet howling on for more vomitest thy wrecks on its inhospitable shore treacherous in calm and terrible in storm who shall put forth on thee unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 1 <\s>
<s> far far away o ye halcyons of memory seek some far calmer nest than this abandoned breast <\s>
<s> no news of your false spring 5 to my heart's winter bring once having gone in vain ye come again <\s>
<s> vultures who build your bowers high in the future's towers 10 withered hopes on hopes are spread <\s>
<s> dying joys choked by the dead will serve your beaks for prey many a day <\s>
<s> from the arabic an imitation <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is an intermediate draft amongst the bodleian manuscripts <\s>
<s> see locock examination etc 1903 page 13 1 <\s>
<s> my faint spirit was sitting in the light of thy looks my love it panted for thee like the hind at noon for the brooks my love <\s>
<s> thy barb whose hoofs outspeed the tempest's flight 5 bore thee far from me my heart for my weak feet were weary soon did companion thee <\s>
<s> fleeter far than fleetest storm or steed or the death they bear 10 the heart which tender thought clothes like a dove with the wings of care in the battle in the darkness in the need shall mine cling to thee nor claim one smile for all the comfort love 15 it may bring to thee <\s>
<s> notes 3 hoofs feet b <\s>
<s> 7 were grew b <\s>
<s> 9 ah o b <\s>
<s> published 1 by mrs <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 2 1 by dr <\s>
<s> garnett relics of shelley 1862 2 2 and 3 by h <\s>
<s> buxton forman poetical works of p <\s>
<s> madonna wherefore hast thou sent to me sweet basil and mignonette <\s>
<s> embleming love and health which never yet in the same wreath might be <\s>
<s> alas and they are wet <\s>
<s> 5 is it with thy kisses or thy tears <\s>
<s> for never rain or dew such fragrance drew from plant or flower the very doubt endears my sadness ever new 10 the sighs i breathe the tears i shed for thee <\s>
<s> send the stars light but send not love to me in whom love ever made health like a heap of embers soon to fade the fugitives <\s>
<s> the waters are flashing the white hail is dashing the lightnings are glancing the hoar spray is dancing away <\s>
<s> 5 the whirlwind is rolling the thunder is tolling the forest is swinging the minster bells ringing come away <\s>
<s> 10 the earth is like ocean wreck strewn and in motion bird beast man and worm have crept out of the storm come away <\s>
<s> our boat has one sail and the helmsman is pale a bold pilot i trow who should follow us now shouted he 20 and she cried ply the oar <\s>
<s> put off gaily from shore as she spoke bolts of death mixed with hail specked their path o'er the sea <\s>
<s> 25 and from isle tower and rock the blue beacon cloud broke and though dumb in the blast the red cannon flashed fast from the lee <\s>
<s> and drive we not free o'er the terrible sea i and thou <\s>
<s> 35 one boat cloak did cover the loved and the lover their blood beats one measure they murmur proud pleasure soft and low 40 while around the lashed ocean like mountains in motion is withdrawn and uplifted sunk shattered and shifted to and fro <\s>
<s> in the court of the fortress beside the pale portress like a bloodhound well beaten the bridegroom stands eaten by shame 50 on the topmost watch turret as a death boding spirit stands the gray tyrant father to his voice the mad weather seems tame 55 and with curses as wild as e'er clung to child he devotes to the blast the best loveliest and last of his name <\s>
<s> 60 notes 28 and though though editions 1839 <\s>
<s> 57 clung cling editions 1839 <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 music when soft voices die vibrates in the memory odours when sweet violets sicken live within the sense they quicken <\s>
<s> rose leaves when the rose is dead 5 are heaped for the beloved's bed and so thy thoughts when thou art gone love itself shall slumber on <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> rarely rarely comest thou spirit of delight <\s>
<s> wherefore hast thou left me now many a day and night <\s>
<s> many a weary night and day 5 tis since thou art fled away <\s>
<s> how shall ever one like me win thee back again <\s>
<s> with the joyous and the free thou wilt scoff at pain <\s>
<s> thou hast forgot all but those who need thee not <\s>
<s> as a lizard with the shade of a trembling leaf thou with sorrow art dismayed 15 even the sighs of grief reproach thee that thou art not near and reproach thou wilt not hear <\s>
<s> let me set my mournful ditty to a merry measure 20 thou wilt never come for pity thou wilt come for pleasure pity then will cut away those cruel wings and thou wilt stay <\s>
<s> i love all that thou lovest 25 spirit of delight <\s>
<s> the fresh earth in new leaves dressed and the starry night autumn evening and the morn when the golden mists are born <\s>
<s> i love snow and all the forms of the radiant frost i love waves and winds and storms everything almost which is nature's and may be 35 untainted by man's misery <\s>
<s> i love tranquil solitude and such society as is quiet wise and good between thee and me 40 what difference <\s>
<s> but thou dost possess the things i seek not love them less <\s>
<s> i love love though he has wings and like light can flee but above all other things 45 spirit i love thee thou art love and life <\s>
<s> oh come make once more my heart thy home <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a fair draft amongst the boscombe manuscripts 1 <\s>
<s> the flower that smiles to day to morrow dies all that we wish to stay tempts and then flies <\s>
<s> what is this world's delight <\s>
<s> 5 lightning that mocks the night brief even as bright <\s>
<s> virtue how frail it is <\s>
<s> love how it sells poor bliss 10 for proud despair <\s>
<s> but we though soon they fall survive their joy and all which ours we call <\s>
<s> the canal overflowed in the garden behind the rising waters on either side at last burst open the doors and meeting in the house rose to the height of six feet <\s>
<s> it was a picturesque sight at night to see the peasants driving the cattle from the plains below to the hills above the baths <\s>
<s> a fire was kept up to guide them across the ford and the forms of the men and the animals showed in dark relief against the red glare of the flame which was reflected again in the waters that filled the square <\s>
<s> we then removed to pisa and took up our abode there for the winter <\s>
<s> the extreme mildness of the climate suited shelley and his solitude was enlivened by an intercourse with several intimate friends <\s>
<s> chance cast us strangely enough on this quiet half unpeopled town but its very peace suited shelley <\s>
<s> its river the near mountains and not distant sea added to its attractions and were the objects of many delightful excursions <\s>
<s> we feared the south of italy and a hotter climate on account of our child our former bereavement inspiring us with terror <\s>
<s> we seemed to take root here and moved little afterwards often indeed entertaining projects for visiting other parts of italy but still delaying <\s>
<s> but for our fears on account of our child i believe we should have wandered over the world both being passionately fond of travelling <\s>
<s> but human life besides its great unalterable necessities is ruled by a thousand lilliputian ties that shackle at the time although it is difficult to account afterwards for their influence over our destiny <\s>
<s> poems written in 1821 <\s>
<s> dirge for the year <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 and dated january 1 1821 1 <\s>
<s> orphan hours the year is dead come and sigh come and weep <\s>
<s> merry hours smile instead for the year is but asleep <\s>
<s> see it smiles as it is sleeping 5 mocking your untimely weeping <\s>
<s> as an earthquake rocks a corse in its coffin in the clay so white winter that rough nurse rocks the death cold year to day 10 solemn hours <\s>
<s> wail aloud for your mother in her shroud <\s>
<s> as the wild air stirs and sways the tree swung cradle of a child so the breath of these rude days 15 rocks the year be calm and mild trembling hours she will arise with new love within her eyes <\s>
<s> january gray is here like a sexton by her grave 20 february bears the bier march with grief doth howl and rave and april weeps but o ye hours <\s>
<s> follow with may's fairest flowers <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> swiftly walk o'er the western wave spirit of night <\s>
<s> out of the misty eastern cave where all the long and lone daylight thou wovest dreams of joy and fear 5 which make thee terrible and dear swift be thy flight <\s>
<s> wrap thy form in a mantle gray star inwrought <\s>
<s> blind with thine hair the eyes of day 10 kiss her until she be wearied out then wander o'er city and sea and land touching all with thine opiate wand come long sought <\s>
<s> when i arose and saw the dawn 15 i sighed for thee when light rode high and the dew was gone and noon lay heavy on flower and tree and the weary day turned to his rest lingering like an unloved guest i sighed for thee <\s>
<s> thy brother death came and cried wouldst thou me <\s>
<s> thy sweet child sleep the filmy eyed murmured like a noontide bee 25 shall i nestle near thy side <\s>
<s> wouldst thou me and i replied no not thee <\s>
<s> death will come when thou art dead soon too soon 30 sleep will come when thou art fled of neither would i ask the boon i ask of thee beloved night swift be thine approaching flight come soon soon <\s>

<s> orphan hours the year is dead come and sigh come and weep <\s>
<s> merry hours smile instead for the year is but asleep <\s>
<s> see it smiles as it is sleeping 5 mocking your untimely weeping <\s>
<s> as an earthquake rocks a corse in its coffin in the clay so white winter that rough nurse rocks the death cold year to day 10 solemn hours <\s>
<s> wail aloud for your mother in her shroud <\s>
<s> as the wild air stirs and sways the tree swung cradle of a child so the breath of these rude days 15 rocks the year be calm and mild trembling hours she will arise with new love within her eyes <\s>
<s> january gray is here like a sexton by her grave 20 february bears the bier march with grief doth howl and rave and april weeps but o ye hours <\s>
<s> follow with may's fairest flowers <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> swiftly walk o'er the western wave spirit of night <\s>
<s> out of the misty eastern cave where all the long and lone daylight thou wovest dreams of joy and fear 5 which make thee terrible and dear swift be thy flight <\s>
<s> wrap thy form in a mantle gray star inwrought <\s>
<s> blind with thine hair the eyes of day 10 kiss her until she be wearied out then wander o'er city and sea and land touching all with thine opiate wand come long sought <\s>
<s> when i arose and saw the dawn 15 i sighed for thee when light rode high and the dew was gone and noon lay heavy on flower and tree and the weary day turned to his rest lingering like an unloved guest i sighed for thee <\s>
<s> thy brother death came and cried wouldst thou me <\s>
<s> thy sweet child sleep the filmy eyed murmured like a noontide bee 25 shall i nestle near thy side <\s>
<s> wouldst thou me and i replied no not thee <\s>
<s> death will come when thou art dead soon too soon 30 sleep will come when thou art fled of neither would i ask the boon i ask of thee beloved night swift be thine approaching flight come soon soon <\s>
<s> 35 note 1 o'er harvard manuscript over editions 1824 1839 <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> whose waves are years ocean of time whose waters of deep woe are brackish with the salt of human tears <\s>
<s> thou shoreless flood which in thy ebb and flow claspest the limits of mortality 5 and sick of prey yet howling on for more vomitest thy wrecks on its inhospitable shore treacherous in calm and terrible in storm who shall put forth on thee unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 1 <\s>
<s> far far away o ye halcyons of memory seek some far calmer nest than this abandoned breast <\s>
<s> no news of your false spring 5 to my heart's winter bring once having gone in vain ye come again <\s>
<s> vultures who build your bowers high in the future's towers 10 withered hopes on hopes are spread <\s>
<s> dying joys choked by the dead will serve your beaks for prey many a day <\s>
<s> from the arabic an imitation <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is an intermediate draft amongst the bodleian manuscripts <\s>
<s> see locock examination etc 1903 page 13 1 <\s>
<s> my faint spirit was sitting in the light of thy looks my love it panted for thee like the hind at noon for the brooks my love <\s>
<s> thy barb whose hoofs outspeed the tempest's flight 5 bore thee far from me my heart for my weak feet were weary soon did companion thee <\s>
<s> fleeter far than fleetest storm or steed or the death they bear 10 the heart which tender thought clothes like a dove with the wings of care in the battle in the darkness in the need shall mine cling to thee nor claim one smile for all the comfort love 15 it may bring to thee <\s>
<s> notes 3 hoofs feet b <\s>
<s> 7 were grew b <\s>
<s> 9 ah o b <\s>
<s> published 1 by mrs <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 2 1 by dr <\s>
<s> garnett relics of shelley 1862 2 2 and 3 by h <\s>
<s> buxton forman poetical works of p <\s>
<s> madonna wherefore hast thou sent to me sweet basil and mignonette <\s>
<s> embleming love and health which never yet in the same wreath might be <\s>
<s> alas and they are wet <\s>
<s> 5 is it with thy kisses or thy tears <\s>
<s> for never rain or dew such fragrance drew from plant or flower the very doubt endears my sadness ever new 10 the sighs i breathe the tears i shed for thee <\s>
<s> send the stars light but send not love to me in whom love ever made health like a heap of embers soon to fade the fugitives <\s>
<s> the waters are flashing the white hail is dashing the lightnings are glancing the hoar spray is dancing away <\s>
<s> 5 the whirlwind is rolling the thunder is tolling the forest is swinging the minster bells ringing come away <\s>
<s> 10 the earth is like ocean wreck strewn and in motion bird beast man and worm have crept out of the storm come away <\s>
<s> our boat has one sail and the helmsman is pale a bold pilot i trow who should follow us now shouted he 20 and she cried ply the oar <\s>
<s> put off gaily from shore as she spoke bolts of death mixed with hail specked their path o'er the sea <\s>
<s> 25 and from isle tower and rock the blue beacon cloud broke and though dumb in the blast the red cannon flashed fast from the lee <\s>
<s> and drive we not free o'er the terrible sea i and thou <\s>
<s> 35 one boat cloak did cover the loved and the lover their blood beats one measure they murmur proud pleasure soft and low 40 while around the lashed ocean like mountains in motion is withdrawn and uplifted sunk shattered and shifted to and fro <\s>
<s> in the court of the fortress beside the pale portress like a bloodhound well beaten the bridegroom stands eaten by shame 50 on the topmost watch turret as a death boding spirit stands the gray tyrant father to his voice the mad weather seems tame 55 and with curses as wild as e'er clung to child he devotes to the blast the best loveliest and last of his name <\s>
<s> 60 notes 28 and though though editions 1839 <\s>
<s> 57 clung cling editions 1839 <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 music when soft voices die vibrates in the memory odours when sweet violets sicken live within the sense they quicken <\s>
<s> rose leaves when the rose is dead 5 are heaped for the beloved's bed and so thy thoughts when thou art gone love itself shall slumber on <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> rarely rarely comest thou spirit of delight <\s>
<s> wherefore hast thou left me now many a day and night <\s>
<s> many a weary night and day 5 tis since thou art fled away <\s>
<s> how shall ever one like me win thee back again <\s>
<s> with the joyous and the free thou wilt scoff at pain <\s>
<s> thou hast forgot all but those who need thee not <\s>
<s> as a lizard with the shade of a trembling leaf thou with sorrow art dismayed 15 even the sighs of grief reproach thee that thou art not near and reproach thou wilt not hear <\s>
<s> let me set my mournful ditty to a merry measure 20 thou wilt never come for pity thou wilt come for pleasure pity then will cut away those cruel wings and thou wilt stay <\s>
<s> i love all that thou lovest 25 spirit of delight <\s>
<s> the fresh earth in new leaves dressed and the starry night autumn evening and the morn when the golden mists are born <\s>
<s> i love snow and all the forms of the radiant frost i love waves and winds and storms everything almost which is nature's and may be 35 untainted by man's misery <\s>
<s> i love tranquil solitude and such society as is quiet wise and good between thee and me 40 what difference <\s>
<s> but thou dost possess the things i seek not love them less <\s>
<s> i love love though he has wings and like light can flee but above all other things 45 spirit i love thee thou art love and life <\s>
<s> oh come make once more my heart thy home <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a fair draft amongst the boscombe manuscripts 1 <\s>
<s> the flower that smiles to day to morrow dies all that we wish to stay tempts and then flies <\s>
<s> what is this world's delight <\s>
<s> 5 lightning that mocks the night brief even as bright <\s>
<s> virtue how frail it is <\s>
<s> love how it sells poor bliss 10 for proud despair <\s>
<s> but we though soon they fall survive their joy and all which ours we call <\s>
<s> the canal overflowed in the garden behind the rising waters on either side at last burst open the doors and meeting in the house rose to the height of six feet <\s>
<s> it was a picturesque sight at night to see the peasants driving the cattle from the plains below to the hills above the baths <\s>
<s> a fire was kept up to guide them across the ford and the forms of the men and the animals showed in dark relief against the red glare of the flame which was reflected again in the waters that filled the square <\s>
<s> we then removed to pisa and took up our abode there for the winter <\s>
<s> the extreme mildness of the climate suited shelley and his solitude was enlivened by an intercourse with several intimate friends <\s>
<s> chance cast us strangely enough on this quiet half unpeopled town but its very peace suited shelley <\s>
<s> its river the near mountains and not distant sea added to its attractions and were the objects of many delightful excursions <\s>
<s> we feared the south of italy and a hotter climate on account of our child our former bereavement inspiring us with terror <\s>
<s> we seemed to take root here and moved little afterwards often indeed entertaining projects for visiting other parts of italy but still delaying <\s>
<s> but for our fears on account of our child i believe we should have wandered over the world both being passionately fond of travelling <\s>
<s> but human life besides its great unalterable necessities is ruled by a thousand lilliputian ties that shackle at the time although it is difficult to account afterwards for their influence over our destiny <\s>

<s> oh come make once more my heart thy home <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a fair draft amongst the boscombe manuscripts 1 <\s>
<s> the flower that smiles to day to morrow dies all that we wish to stay tempts and then flies <\s>
<s> what is this world's delight <\s>
<s> 5 lightning that mocks the night brief even as bright <\s>
<s> virtue how frail it is <\s>
<s> love how it sells poor bliss 10 for proud despair <\s>
<s> but we though soon they fall survive their joy and all which ours we call <\s>
<s> the canal overflowed in the garden behind the rising waters on either side at last burst open the doors and meeting in the house rose to the height of six feet <\s>
<s> it was a picturesque sight at night to see the peasants driving the cattle from the plains below to the hills above the baths <\s>
<s> a fire was kept up to guide them across the ford and the forms of the men and the animals showed in dark relief against the red glare of the flame which was reflected again in the waters that filled the square <\s>
<s> we then removed to pisa and took up our abode there for the winter <\s>
<s> the extreme mildness of the climate suited shelley and his solitude was enlivened by an intercourse with several intimate friends <\s>
<s> chance cast us strangely enough on this quiet half unpeopled town but its very peace suited shelley <\s>
<s> its river the near mountains and not distant sea added to its attractions and were the objects of many delightful excursions <\s>
<s> we feared the south of italy and a hotter climate on account of our child our former bereavement inspiring us with terror <\s>
<s> we seemed to take root here and moved little afterwards often indeed entertaining projects for visiting other parts of italy but still delaying <\s>
<s> but for our fears on account of our child i believe we should have wandered over the world both being passionately fond of travelling <\s>
<s> but human life besides its great unalterable necessities is ruled by a thousand lilliputian ties that shackle at the time although it is difficult to account afterwards for their influence over our destiny <\s>
<s> poems written in 1821 <\s>
<s> dirge for the year <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 and dated january 1 1821 1 <\s>
<s> orphan hours the year is dead come and sigh come and weep <\s>
<s> merry hours smile instead for the year is but asleep <\s>
<s> see it smiles as it is sleeping 5 mocking your untimely weeping <\s>
<s> as an earthquake rocks a corse in its coffin in the clay so white winter that rough nurse rocks the death cold year to day 10 solemn hours <\s>
<s> wail aloud for your mother in her shroud <\s>
<s> as the wild air stirs and sways the tree swung cradle of a child so the breath of these rude days 15 rocks the year be calm and mild trembling hours she will arise with new love within her eyes <\s>
<s> january gray is here like a sexton by her grave 20 february bears the bier march with grief doth howl and rave and april weeps but o ye hours <\s>
<s> follow with may's fairest flowers <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> swiftly walk o'er the western wave spirit of night <\s>
<s> out of the misty eastern cave where all the long and lone daylight thou wovest dreams of joy and fear 5 which make thee terrible and dear swift be thy flight <\s>
<s> wrap thy form in a mantle gray star inwrought <\s>
<s> blind with thine hair the eyes of day 10 kiss her until she be wearied out then wander o'er city and sea and land touching all with thine opiate wand come long sought <\s>
<s> when i arose and saw the dawn 15 i sighed for thee when light rode high and the dew was gone and noon lay heavy on flower and tree and the weary day turned to his rest lingering like an unloved guest i sighed for thee <\s>
<s> thy brother death came and cried wouldst thou me <\s>
<s> thy sweet child sleep the filmy eyed murmured like a noontide bee 25 shall i nestle near thy side <\s>
<s> wouldst thou me and i replied no not thee <\s>
<s> death will come when thou art dead soon too soon 30 sleep will come when thou art fled of neither would i ask the boon i ask of thee beloved night swift be thine approaching flight come soon soon <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> whose waves are years ocean of time whose waters of deep woe are brackish with the salt of human tears <\s>
<s> thou shoreless flood which in thy ebb and flow claspest the limits of mortality 5 and sick of prey yet howling on for more vomitest thy wrecks on its inhospitable shore treacherous in calm and terrible in storm who shall put forth on thee unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 1 <\s>
<s> far far away o ye halcyons of memory seek some far calmer nest than this abandoned breast <\s>
<s> no news of your false spring 5 to my heart's winter bring once having gone in vain ye come again <\s>
<s> vultures who build your bowers high in the future's towers 10 withered hopes on hopes are spread <\s>
<s> dying joys choked by the dead will serve your beaks for prey many a day <\s>
<s> from the arabic an imitation <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is an intermediate draft amongst the bodleian manuscripts <\s>
<s> see locock examination etc 1903 page 13 1 <\s>
<s> my faint spirit was sitting in the light of thy looks my love it panted for thee like the hind at noon for the brooks my love <\s>
<s> thy barb whose hoofs outspeed the tempest's flight 5 bore thee far from me my heart for my weak feet were weary soon did companion thee <\s>
<s> fleeter far than fleetest storm or steed or the death they bear 10 the heart which tender thought clothes like a dove with the wings of care in the battle in the darkness in the need shall mine cling to thee nor claim one smile for all the comfort love 15 it may bring to thee <\s>

<s> buxton forman poetical works of p <\s>
<s> madonna wherefore hast thou sent to me sweet basil and mignonette <\s>
<s> embleming love and health which never yet in the same wreath might be <\s>
<s> alas and they are wet <\s>
<s> 5 is it with thy kisses or thy tears <\s>
<s> for never rain or dew such fragrance drew from plant or flower the very doubt endears my sadness ever new 10 the sighs i breathe the tears i shed for thee <\s>
<s> send the stars light but send not love to me in whom love ever made health like a heap of embers soon to fade the fugitives <\s>
<s> the waters are flashing the white hail is dashing the lightnings are glancing the hoar spray is dancing away <\s>
<s> 5 the whirlwind is rolling the thunder is tolling the forest is swinging the minster bells ringing come away <\s>
<s> 10 the earth is like ocean wreck strewn and in motion bird beast man and worm have crept out of the storm come away <\s>
<s> our boat has one sail and the helmsman is pale a bold pilot i trow who should follow us now shouted he 20 and she cried ply the oar <\s>
<s> put off gaily from shore as she spoke bolts of death mixed with hail specked their path o'er the sea <\s>
<s> 25 and from isle tower and rock the blue beacon cloud broke and though dumb in the blast the red cannon flashed fast from the lee <\s>
<s> and drive we not free o'er the terrible sea i and thou <\s>
<s> 35 one boat cloak did cover the loved and the lover their blood beats one measure they murmur proud pleasure soft and low 40 while around the lashed ocean like mountains in motion is withdrawn and uplifted sunk shattered and shifted to and fro <\s>
<s> in the court of the fortress beside the pale portress like a bloodhound well beaten the bridegroom stands eaten by shame 50 on the topmost watch turret as a death boding spirit stands the gray tyrant father to his voice the mad weather seems tame 55 and with curses as wild as e'er clung to child he devotes to the blast the best loveliest and last of his name <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 music when soft voices die vibrates in the memory odours when sweet violets sicken live within the sense they quicken <\s>
<s> rose leaves when the rose is dead 5 are heaped for the beloved's bed and so thy thoughts when thou art gone love itself shall slumber on <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> rarely rarely comest thou spirit of delight <\s>
<s> wherefore hast thou left me now many a day and night <\s>
<s> many a weary night and day 5 tis since thou art fled away <\s>
<s> how shall ever one like me win thee back again <\s>
<s> with the joyous and the free thou wilt scoff at pain <\s>
<s> thou hast forgot all but those who need thee not <\s>
<s> as a lizard with the shade of a trembling leaf thou with sorrow art dismayed 15 even the sighs of grief reproach thee that thou art not near and reproach thou wilt not hear <\s>
<s> let me set my mournful ditty to a merry measure 20 thou wilt never come for pity thou wilt come for pleasure pity then will cut away those cruel wings and thou wilt stay <\s>
<s> i love all that thou lovest 25 spirit of delight <\s>
<s> the fresh earth in new leaves dressed and the starry night autumn evening and the morn when the golden mists are born <\s>
<s> i love snow and all the forms of the radiant frost i love waves and winds and storms everything almost which is nature's and may be 35 untainted by man's misery <\s>
<s> i love tranquil solitude and such society as is quiet wise and good between thee and me 40 what difference <\s>
<s> but thou dost possess the things i seek not love them less <\s>
<s> i love love though he has wings and like light can flee but above all other things 45 spirit i love thee thou art love and life <\s>
<s> oh come make once more my heart thy home <\s>

<s> in the court of the fortress beside the pale portress like a bloodhound well beaten the bridegroom stands eaten by shame 50 on the topmost watch turret as a death boding spirit stands the gray tyrant father to his voice the mad weather seems tame 55 and with curses as wild as e'er clung to child he devotes to the blast the best loveliest and last of his name <\s>
<s> 60 notes 28 and though though editions 1839 <\s>
<s> 57 clung cling editions 1839 <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 music when soft voices die vibrates in the memory odours when sweet violets sicken live within the sense they quicken <\s>
<s> rose leaves when the rose is dead 5 are heaped for the beloved's bed and so thy thoughts when thou art gone love itself shall slumber on <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> rarely rarely comest thou spirit of delight <\s>
<s> wherefore hast thou left me now many a day and night <\s>
<s> many a weary night and day 5 tis since thou art fled away <\s>
<s> how shall ever one like me win thee back again <\s>
<s> with the joyous and the free thou wilt scoff at pain <\s>
<s> thou hast forgot all but those who need thee not <\s>
<s> as a lizard with the shade of a trembling leaf thou with sorrow art dismayed 15 even the sighs of grief reproach thee that thou art not near and reproach thou wilt not hear <\s>
<s> let me set my mournful ditty to a merry measure 20 thou wilt never come for pity thou wilt come for pleasure pity then will cut away those cruel wings and thou wilt stay <\s>
<s> i love all that thou lovest 25 spirit of delight <\s>
<s> the fresh earth in new leaves dressed and the starry night autumn evening and the morn when the golden mists are born <\s>
<s> i love snow and all the forms of the radiant frost i love waves and winds and storms everything almost which is nature's and may be 35 untainted by man's misery <\s>
<s> i love tranquil solitude and such society as is quiet wise and good between thee and me 40 what difference <\s>
<s> but thou dost possess the things i seek not love them less <\s>
<s> i love love though he has wings and like light can flee but above all other things 45 spirit i love thee thou art love and life <\s>
<s> oh come make once more my heart thy home <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a fair draft amongst the boscombe manuscripts 1 <\s>
<s> the flower that smiles to day to morrow dies all that we wish to stay tempts and then flies <\s>
<s> what is this world's delight <\s>
<s> 5 lightning that mocks the night brief even as bright <\s>
<s> virtue how frail it is <\s>
<s> love how it sells poor bliss 10 for proud despair <\s>
<s> but we though soon they fall survive their joy and all which ours we call <\s>
<s> the canal overflowed in the garden behind the rising waters on either side at last burst open the doors and meeting in the house rose to the height of six feet <\s>
<s> it was a picturesque sight at night to see the peasants driving the cattle from the plains below to the hills above the baths <\s>
<s> a fire was kept up to guide them across the ford and the forms of the men and the animals showed in dark relief against the red glare of the flame which was reflected again in the waters that filled the square <\s>
<s> we then removed to pisa and took up our abode there for the winter <\s>
<s> the extreme mildness of the climate suited shelley and his solitude was enlivened by an intercourse with several intimate friends <\s>
<s> chance cast us strangely enough on this quiet half unpeopled town but its very peace suited shelley <\s>
<s> its river the near mountains and not distant sea added to its attractions and were the objects of many delightful excursions <\s>
<s> we feared the south of italy and a hotter climate on account of our child our former bereavement inspiring us with terror <\s>
<s> we seemed to take root here and moved little afterwards often indeed entertaining projects for visiting other parts of italy but still delaying <\s>
<s> but for our fears on account of our child i believe we should have wandered over the world both being passionately fond of travelling <\s>
<s> but human life besides its great unalterable necessities is ruled by a thousand lilliputian ties that shackle at the time although it is difficult to account afterwards for their influence over our destiny <\s>
<s> poems written in 1821 <\s>
<s> dirge for the year <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 and dated january 1 1821 1 <\s>
<s> orphan hours the year is dead come and sigh come and weep <\s>
<s> merry hours smile instead for the year is but asleep <\s>
<s> see it smiles as it is sleeping 5 mocking your untimely weeping <\s>
<s> as an earthquake rocks a corse in its coffin in the clay so white winter that rough nurse rocks the death cold year to day 10 solemn hours <\s>
<s> wail aloud for your mother in her shroud <\s>
<s> as the wild air stirs and sways the tree swung cradle of a child so the breath of these rude days 15 rocks the year be calm and mild trembling hours she will arise with new love within her eyes <\s>
<s> january gray is here like a sexton by her grave 20 february bears the bier march with grief doth howl and rave and april weeps but o ye hours <\s>
<s> follow with may's fairest flowers <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> swiftly walk o'er the western wave spirit of night <\s>
<s> out of the misty eastern cave where all the long and lone daylight thou wovest dreams of joy and fear 5 which make thee terrible and dear swift be thy flight <\s>
<s> wrap thy form in a mantle gray star inwrought <\s>
<s> blind with thine hair the eyes of day 10 kiss her until she be wearied out then wander o'er city and sea and land touching all with thine opiate wand come long sought <\s>
<s> when i arose and saw the dawn 15 i sighed for thee when light rode high and the dew was gone and noon lay heavy on flower and tree and the weary day turned to his rest lingering like an unloved guest i sighed for thee <\s>
<s> thy brother death came and cried wouldst thou me <\s>
<s> thy sweet child sleep the filmy eyed murmured like a noontide bee 25 shall i nestle near thy side <\s>
<s> wouldst thou me and i replied no not thee <\s>
<s> death will come when thou art dead soon too soon 30 sleep will come when thou art fled of neither would i ask the boon i ask of thee beloved night swift be thine approaching flight come soon soon <\s>
<s> 35 note 1 o'er harvard manuscript over editions 1824 1839 <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> whose waves are years ocean of time whose waters of deep woe are brackish with the salt of human tears <\s>
<s> thou shoreless flood which in thy ebb and flow claspest the limits of mortality 5 and sick of prey yet howling on for more vomitest thy wrecks on its inhospitable shore treacherous in calm and terrible in storm who shall put forth on thee unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 1 <\s>
<s> far far away o ye halcyons of memory seek some far calmer nest than this abandoned breast <\s>
<s> no news of your false spring 5 to my heart's winter bring once having gone in vain ye come again <\s>
<s> vultures who build your bowers high in the future's towers 10 withered hopes on hopes are spread <\s>
<s> dying joys choked by the dead will serve your beaks for prey many a day <\s>
<s> from the arabic an imitation <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is an intermediate draft amongst the bodleian manuscripts <\s>
<s> see locock examination etc 1903 page 13 1 <\s>
<s> my faint spirit was sitting in the light of thy looks my love it panted for thee like the hind at noon for the brooks my love <\s>
<s> thy barb whose hoofs outspeed the tempest's flight 5 bore thee far from me my heart for my weak feet were weary soon did companion thee <\s>
<s> fleeter far than fleetest storm or steed or the death they bear 10 the heart which tender thought clothes like a dove with the wings of care in the battle in the darkness in the need shall mine cling to thee nor claim one smile for all the comfort love 15 it may bring to thee <\s>

<s> embleming love and health which never yet in the same wreath might be <\s>
<s> alas and they are wet <\s>
<s> 5 is it with thy kisses or thy tears <\s>
<s> for never rain or dew such fragrance drew from plant or flower the very doubt endears my sadness ever new 10 the sighs i breathe the tears i shed for thee <\s>
<s> send the stars light but send not love to me in whom love ever made health like a heap of embers soon to fade the fugitives <\s>
<s> the waters are flashing the white hail is dashing the lightnings are glancing the hoar spray is dancing away <\s>
<s> 5 the whirlwind is rolling the thunder is tolling the forest is swinging the minster bells ringing come away <\s>
<s> 10 the earth is like ocean wreck strewn and in motion bird beast man and worm have crept out of the storm come away <\s>
<s> our boat has one sail and the helmsman is pale a bold pilot i trow who should follow us now shouted he 20 and she cried ply the oar <\s>
<s> put off gaily from shore as she spoke bolts of death mixed with hail specked their path o'er the sea <\s>
<s> 25 and from isle tower and rock the blue beacon cloud broke and though dumb in the blast the red cannon flashed fast from the lee <\s>

<s> thy barb whose hoofs outspeed the tempest's flight 5 bore thee far from me my heart for my weak feet were weary soon did companion thee <\s>
<s> fleeter far than fleetest storm or steed or the death they bear 10 the heart which tender thought clothes like a dove with the wings of care in the battle in the darkness in the need shall mine cling to thee nor claim one smile for all the comfort love 15 it may bring to thee <\s>

<s> buxton forman poetical works of p <\s>
<s> madonna wherefore hast thou sent to me sweet basil and mignonette <\s>
<s> embleming love and health which never yet in the same wreath might be <\s>
<s> alas and they are wet <\s>
<s> 5 is it with thy kisses or thy tears <\s>
<s> for never rain or dew such fragrance drew from plant or flower the very doubt endears my sadness ever new 10 the sighs i breathe the tears i shed for thee <\s>
<s> send the stars light but send not love to me in whom love ever made health like a heap of embers soon to fade the fugitives <\s>
<s> the waters are flashing the white hail is dashing the lightnings are glancing the hoar spray is dancing away <\s>
<s> 5 the whirlwind is rolling the thunder is tolling the forest is swinging the minster bells ringing come away <\s>
<s> 10 the earth is like ocean wreck strewn and in motion bird beast man and worm have crept out of the storm come away <\s>
<s> our boat has one sail and the helmsman is pale a bold pilot i trow who should follow us now shouted he 20 and she cried ply the oar <\s>
<s> put off gaily from shore as she spoke bolts of death mixed with hail specked their path o'er the sea <\s>
<s> 25 and from isle tower and rock the blue beacon cloud broke and though dumb in the blast the red cannon flashed fast from the lee <\s>
<s> and drive we not free o'er the terrible sea i and thou <\s>
<s> 35 one boat cloak did cover the loved and the lover their blood beats one measure they murmur proud pleasure soft and low 40 while around the lashed ocean like mountains in motion is withdrawn and uplifted sunk shattered and shifted to and fro <\s>
<s> in the court of the fortress beside the pale portress like a bloodhound well beaten the bridegroom stands eaten by shame 50 on the topmost watch turret as a death boding spirit stands the gray tyrant father to his voice the mad weather seems tame 55 and with curses as wild as e'er clung to child he devotes to the blast the best loveliest and last of his name <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 music when soft voices die vibrates in the memory odours when sweet violets sicken live within the sense they quicken <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> rarely rarely comest thou spirit of delight <\s>
<s> wherefore hast thou left me now many a day and night <\s>
<s> many a weary night and day 5 tis since thou art fled away <\s>
<s> how shall ever one like me win thee back again <\s>
<s> with the joyous and the free thou wilt scoff at pain <\s>
<s> thou hast forgot all but those who need thee not <\s>
<s> as a lizard with the shade of a trembling leaf thou with sorrow art dismayed 15 even the sighs of grief reproach thee that thou art not near and reproach thou wilt not hear <\s>
<s> let me set my mournful ditty to a merry measure 20 thou wilt never come for pity thou wilt come for pleasure pity then will cut away those cruel wings and thou wilt stay <\s>
<s> i love all that thou lovest 25 spirit of delight <\s>
<s> the fresh earth in new leaves dressed and the starry night autumn evening and the morn when the golden mists are born <\s>
<s> i love snow and all the forms of the radiant frost i love waves and winds and storms everything almost which is nature's and may be 35 untainted by man's misery <\s>
<s> i love tranquil solitude and such society as is quiet wise and good between thee and me 40 what difference <\s>
<s> but thou dost possess the things i seek not love them less <\s>
<s> i love love though he has wings and like light can flee but above all other things 45 spirit i love thee thou art love and life <\s>
<s> oh come make once more my heart thy home <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a fair draft amongst the boscombe manuscripts 1 <\s>
<s> the flower that smiles to day to morrow dies all that we wish to stay tempts and then flies <\s>
<s> what is this world's delight <\s>
<s> 5 lightning that mocks the night brief even as bright <\s>
<s> virtue how frail it is <\s>
<s> love how it sells poor bliss 10 for proud despair <\s>
<s> but we though soon they fall survive their joy and all which ours we call <\s>
<s> the canal overflowed in the garden behind the rising waters on either side at last burst open the doors and meeting in the house rose to the height of six feet <\s>
<s> it was a picturesque sight at night to see the peasants driving the cattle from the plains below to the hills above the baths <\s>
<s> a fire was kept up to guide them across the ford and the forms of the men and the animals showed in dark relief against the red glare of the flame which was reflected again in the waters that filled the square <\s>
<s> we then removed to pisa and took up our abode there for the winter <\s>
<s> the extreme mildness of the climate suited shelley and his solitude was enlivened by an intercourse with several intimate friends <\s>
<s> chance cast us strangely enough on this quiet half unpeopled town but its very peace suited shelley <\s>
<s> its river the near mountains and not distant sea added to its attractions and were the objects of many delightful excursions <\s>
<s> we feared the south of italy and a hotter climate on account of our child our former bereavement inspiring us with terror <\s>
<s> we seemed to take root here and moved little afterwards often indeed entertaining projects for visiting other parts of italy but still delaying <\s>
<s> but for our fears on account of our child i believe we should have wandered over the world both being passionately fond of travelling <\s>
<s> but human life besides its great unalterable necessities is ruled by a thousand lilliputian ties that shackle at the time although it is difficult to account afterwards for their influence over our destiny <\s>
<s> poems written in 1821 <\s>
<s> dirge for the year <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 and dated january 1 1821 1 <\s>
<s> orphan hours the year is dead come and sigh come and weep <\s>
<s> merry hours smile instead for the year is but asleep <\s>
<s> see it smiles as it is sleeping 5 mocking your untimely weeping <\s>
<s> as an earthquake rocks a corse in its coffin in the clay so white winter that rough nurse rocks the death cold year to day 10 solemn hours <\s>
<s> wail aloud for your mother in her shroud <\s>
<s> as the wild air stirs and sways the tree swung cradle of a child so the breath of these rude days 15 rocks the year be calm and mild trembling hours she will arise with new love within her eyes <\s>
<s> january gray is here like a sexton by her grave 20 february bears the bier march with grief doth howl and rave and april weeps but o ye hours <\s>
<s> follow with may's fairest flowers <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript in the harvard manuscript book 1 <\s>
<s> swiftly walk o'er the western wave spirit of night <\s>
<s> out of the misty eastern cave where all the long and lone daylight thou wovest dreams of joy and fear 5 which make thee terrible and dear swift be thy flight <\s>
<s> wrap thy form in a mantle gray star inwrought <\s>
<s> blind with thine hair the eyes of day 10 kiss her until she be wearied out then wander o'er city and sea and land touching all with thine opiate wand come long sought <\s>
<s> when i arose and saw the dawn 15 i sighed for thee when light rode high and the dew was gone and noon lay heavy on flower and tree and the weary day turned to his rest lingering like an unloved guest i sighed for thee <\s>
<s> thy brother death came and cried wouldst thou me <\s>
<s> thy sweet child sleep the filmy eyed murmured like a noontide bee 25 shall i nestle near thy side <\s>
<s> wouldst thou me and i replied no not thee <\s>
<s> death will come when thou art dead soon too soon 30 sleep will come when thou art fled of neither would i ask the boon i ask of thee beloved night swift be thine approaching flight come soon soon <\s>
<s> 35 note 1 o'er harvard manuscript over editions 1824 1839 <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> whose waves are years ocean of time whose waters of deep woe are brackish with the salt of human tears <\s>
<s> thou shoreless flood which in thy ebb and flow claspest the limits of mortality 5 and sick of prey yet howling on for more vomitest thy wrecks on its inhospitable shore treacherous in calm and terrible in storm who shall put forth on thee unfathomable sea <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 1 <\s>
<s> far far away o ye halcyons of memory seek some far calmer nest than this abandoned breast <\s>
<s> no news of your false spring 5 to my heart's winter bring once having gone in vain ye come again <\s>
<s> vultures who build your bowers high in the future's towers 10 withered hopes on hopes are spread <\s>
<s> dying joys choked by the dead will serve your beaks for prey many a day <\s>
<s> from the arabic an imitation <\s>
